# JLPT N Data file for zkanji.
#
# The data was compiled from official JLPT lists(prior 2010).There are no
# official lists since 2010, but the levels are around the same difficulty.
# A new level N3 was introduced in 2010 as a level between the old 2kyuu and
# 3kyuu. N1 matching 1kyuu, N2 is around 2kyuu, N4 is around 3kyuu, and N5 is
# like 4kyuu. The data for the missing N3 comes from a part of 2kyuu, and is
# based entirely on early textbooks from 2010 and my assumptions, which were
# based on word frequency, official example questions for N3 and words about
# topics that come up in the JLPT.
#
# DISCLAIMER: this data is provided AS IS. It contains errors. There is no
# guarantee that the new N levels use anything from the old JLPT. You might
# fail the exam even if you learn everything from this list. Use this data
# at your own risk. I take no responsibility if you don't pass the test.
#
# Format:
#   Lines starting with # are comments.
#   JLPT N data for words lasts till the first empty line.
#   Each word data contains three fields separated by TAB.
#   The fields are:
#     kanji form
#     kana reading
#     N level
#   JLPT N data for kanji starts after the first empty line till the
#   end of file.
#   The kanji N data contains 2 fields with no space between them:
#     kanji character.
#     N level
#
